Reader guide

You are viewing the SNU update log. This log documents the development of the SNU website from xxxxxxx.2017 to the current day

The log is divided into several sections, the megasections are the years, which contain the sections for the months the site was developed. In each month, there are daily logs for each time the website was modified

The formatting of these is not meant for just casual reading, it was made to document the development cycle of the entire websites codebase.

The page is written so the newest is at the top, and the oldest is at the bottom. Scrolling up will go up in time, scrolling down will go down in time.

Each section is written like a list, the modern day sections include a top description, and a bottom description, which is used as a summary. In between those 2 descriptions is a list

The lists contain 4 types of bullets. The bullet is used to describe a complete change, the - is an older way of describing a single change, the >> is also an older way of describing a single change, and the asterisk * is used to describe a single change within a complete change

Down below each month is a statistical section which counts how many changes there were by the day, by the month, and by the period. It contains a - which leads to the amount of changes that day, following = which counts up this change with all other changes in the month.

There are 2 navigation panes, one at the top of the page, and one in the sidebar. They both contain the same data, you can choose which one you want to use.

These navigation panes link to different days, months, years, and versions of development.

Within the lists, at the end of each listed change, there is a date of when the change occurred, following with a tag that points to which part of the site was being developed.

Articles without a tag need to be manually found, changes will be made to fix the error

There are tags for these sections

[SNU 1D MODE]

[SNU 2D MODE]

[SNU 3D MODE]

[SNU LOBBY DIR]

[SNU P2P SECTION]

[SNU TERMINAL]

These are the main directories of the website. 1D, 2D, and 3D mode are the main users modes, the others are important for the websites database infastructure

Inside the source of the website, there are lots of comments. These give additional information for developers, and as a way of finding sections easier.

The update log is only half of the text recording of SNU development. The other part is the developer log. You can view it here.

You have reached the end of the reader guide. Hopefully you now understand how this page works.

Developer info

You are only viewing half of the text recording of SNU development. The other part is the developer log. You can view it here.

Version 3.0.5 - Changes

Overview

Version 3.0.5 (Version 3 Milestone 6 [M3V6]-) was a major SNU release with over 1100 updates. It is the first release with the twice per year release cycle.

Leading up to the first private release of 3.0.5 (June 14th 2019) the version was constantly mistaken as 3.0.6. The issue was corrected in the last weeks of development of 3.0.4

Also leading up to 3.0.5 was a long range of documentation only updates with little features in anticipation of the wait for 3.0.5, which a main anticipated feature didn't work correctly, and would make a lot more work for nothing, and was cancelled.

Daily updates were made to 3.0.5 from June 14th 2019 to December 14h 2019. At the moment, it is anticipated to release at least 2000 updates to the 3.0.5 branch. As of September 4th 2019, I am already past halfway there.

Planned features

Snapshot folders

A planned feature of SNU 3.0.5 was a snapshot system where new snapshots are stored in a separate folder. This was tested, but turned out as a failure, as the links wouldn't connect correctly once a snapshot is viewed. The change was abandoned.

No other planned features.

Other features

Mass P2P project

Server essentials

3D mode improvements

First SQL usage

Greatly improved interface

Improved documentation

Better update consistency

Starter scripts for ease of page creation

The start of algorithm development

Programming tools improvements

Online shopping system start

Optimizations for public server owners

Virtualization machines (Emularity engine currently abandoned)

1D mode improveents

Enhanced functionality

Legacy content updates

New Internet Museum - the successor to the Legends of the Internet project

Themes added in

Added in TV mode

Added in the SNU DVR into TV mode

Added in the SNU VCR into TV mode

Added in a web crawler/ripper

Began work on an advanced text engine

Heavy updates to programming pages

HTML5 documentation

Added in support for external media servers

Added in a file extension help page center

Added in the slang dictionary

Added in a Wiki

Created snapshot 98 for the SNU developer log - June 14th 2019 [FOR SNU 2D MODE]

Version 3.0.4 - Changes

Overview

Version 3.0.4 (Version 3 Milestone 5 [M3V5]-) was a major SNU release with over 900. It was the first longer term release, with a set update schedule. It was the last version released without a set update schedule (the twice a year schedule) Previous versions were updated when backup was necessary

Version 3.0.3 and previous versions didn't follow and update schedule. Development of 3.0.4 began on February 10th 2019 and ended on June 13th 2019. Version 3.0.5 [M3V6] was released on June 14th 2019 privately.

Planned features

None

Other features

Improved documentation

Page improvements

Snapshots are now an official feature

Version 3.0.4

June 2019 (part 1 of 2)

FINAL 3.0.4 RELEASE!
